   /// Try to acquire an RPM token from the file-based token bucket.\n274\t    ///\n275\t    /// Uses flock for cross-process safety.\n276\t    fn try_acquire_rpm_token(&self, provider: &str, rpm: u32) -> Result<bool> {\n277\t        // Ensure the rate_limits directory exists.\n278\t        std::fs::create_dir_all(&self.state_dir).with_context(|| {\n279\t            format!(\n280\t                \"failed to create rate_limits directory: {}\",\n281\t                self.state_dir.display()\n282\t            )\n283\t        })?;\n284\t\n285\t        let bucket_path = self.state_dir.join(format!(\"{provider}.json\"));\n286\t\n287\t        // Open or create the bucket file.\n288\t        let file = std::fs::OpenOptions::new()\n289\t            .read(true)\n290\t            .write(true)\n291\t            .create(true)\n292\t            .truncate(false)\n293\t            .open(&bucket_path)\n294\t            .with_context(|| {\n295\t                format!(\n296\t                    \"failed to open rate limit bucket: {}\",\n297\t                    bucket_path.display()\n298\t                )\n299\t            })?;\n300\t\n301\t        // Exclusive lock for atomic read-modify-write.\n302\t        FileExt::lock_exclusive(&file).with_context(|| {\n303\t            format!(\n304\t                \"failed to acquire lock on rate limit bucket: {}\",\n305\t                bucket_path.display()\n306\t            )\n307\t        })?;\n308\t\n309\t        // Read current state.\n310\t        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&bucket_path).unwrap_or_default();\n311\t        let mut bucket: TokenBucket = if content.trim().is_empty() {\n312\t            TokenBucket::new(rpm)\n313\t        } else {\n314\t            serde_json::from_str(&content).unwrap_or_else(|_| TokenBucket::new(rpm))\n315\t        };\n316\t\n317\t        // Update capacity if config changed.\n318\t        bucket.capacity = rpm;\n319\t\n320\t        // Try to consume a token.\n321\t        let allowed = bucket.try_consume();\n322\t\n323\t        // Write updated state.\n324\t        let json = serde_json::to_string_pretty(&bucket)\n325\t            .context(\"failed to serialize token bucket state\")?;\n326\t        std::fs::write(&bucket_path, &json).with_context(|| {\n327\t            format!(\n328\t                \"failed to write rate limit bucket: {}\",\n329\t                bucket_path.display()\n330\t            )\n331\t        })?;\n332\t\n333\t        // Release lock.\n334\t        FileExt::unlock(&file).with_context(|| {\n335\t            format!(\n336\t                \"failed to release lock on rate limit bucket: {}\",\n337\t                bucket_path.display()\n338\t            )\n339\t        })?;\n340\t\n341\t        Ok(allowed)\n342\t    }\n343\t\n344\t    /// Check system resource health (CPU load and memory).\n345\t    ///\n346\t    /// Returns warnings as log messages; does not block dispatch.\n347\t    pub fn check_system_resources(cpu_load_warn: f64, memory_free_warn_mb: u64) {\n348\t        // CPU load: read /proc/loadavg on Linux.\n349\t        if let Ok(loadavg) = std::fs::read_to_string(\"/proc/loadavg\") {\n350\t            if let Some(load_str) = loadavg.split_whitespace().next() {\n351\t                if let Ok(load) = load_str.parse::<f64>() {\n352\t                    // Normalize by number of CPUs.\n353\t                    let num_cpus = std::thread::available_parallelism()\n354\t                        .map(|n| n.get() as f64)\n355\t                        .unwrap_or(1.0);\n356\t                    let normalized = load / num_cpus;\n357\t                    if normalized > cpu_load_warn {\n358\t                        tracing::warn!(\n359\t                            load_1min = %load_str,\n360\t                            normalized = %format!(\"{:.2}\", normalized),\n361\t                            threshold = %format!(\"{:.2}\", cpu_load_warn),\n362\t                            \"CPU load exceeds warning threshold\"\n363\t                        );\n364\t                    }\n365\t                }\n366\t            }\n367\t        }\n368\t\n369\t        // Memory: read /proc/meminfo on Linux.\n370\t        if let Ok(meminfo) = std::fs::read_to_string(\"/proc/meminfo\") {\n371\t            let mut mem_available_kb: Option<u64> = None;\n372\t            for line in meminfo.lines() {\n373\t                if line.starts_with(\"MemAvailable:\") {\n374\t                    if let Some(val) = line.split_whitespace().nth(1) {\n375\t                        mem_available_kb = val.parse().ok();\n376\t                    }\n377\t                    break;\n378\t                }\n379\t            }\n380\t            if let Some(avail_kb) = mem_available_kb {\n381\t                let avail_mb = avail_kb / 1024;\n382\t                if avail_mb < memory_free_warn_mb {\n383\t                    tracing::warn!(\n384\t                        available_mb = avail_mb,\n385\t                        threshold_mb = memory_free_warn_mb,\n386\t                        \"available memory below warning threshold\"\n387\t                    );\n388\t                }\n389\t            }\n390\t        }\n391\t    }\n392\t}\n393\t\n394\t// Provider/model concurrency limits and RPM rate limiting.\n//!\n//! Before dispatching an agent, the worker checks:\n//! 1. **Concurrency limits**: Are fewer than `max_concurrent` workers using\n//!    this provider/model? Checked via the worker registry.\n//! 2. **RPM limits**: Has the provider's requests-per-minute budget been\n//!    exceeded? Checked via a file-based token bucket.\n//!\n//! If either check fails, the caller should back off and retry.\n//!\n//! Depends on: `config`, `registry`, `types`.\n\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse anyhow::{Context, Result};\nuse chrono::{DateTime, Utc};\nuse fs2::FileExt;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\n\nuse crate::config::LimitsConfig;\nuse crate::registry::Registry;\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// RateLimitDecision\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Result of a rate limit check.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]\npub enum RateLimitDecision {\n    /// Dispatch is allowed.\n    Allowed,\n    /// Provider concurrency limit reached.\n    ProviderConcurrencyExceeded {\n        provider: String,\n        current: u32,\n        limit: u32,\n    },\n    /// Model concurrency limit reached.\n    ModelConcurrencyExceeded {\n        model: String,\n        current: u32,\n        limit: u32,\n    },\n    /// RPM limit reached for this provider.\n    RpmExceeded {\n        provider: String,\n        requests_per_minute: u32,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl RateLimitDecision {\n    /// Whether dispatch is allowed.\n    pub fn is_allowed(&self) -> bool {\n        matches!(self, RateLimitDecision::Allowed)\n    }\n}\n\nimpl std::fmt::Display for RateLimitDecision {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            RateLimitDecision::Allowed => write!(f, \"allowed\"),\n            RateLimitDecision::ProviderConcurrencyExceeded {\n                provider,\n                current,\n                limit,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"provider '{}' concurrency exceeded ({}/{})\",\n                provider, current, limit\n            ),\n            RateLimitDecision::ModelConcurrencyExceeded {\n                model,\n                current,\n                limit,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"model '{}' concurrency exceeded ({}/{})\",\n                model, current, limit\n            ),\n            RateLimitDecision::RpmExceeded {\n                provider,\n                requests_per_minute,\n            } => write!(\n                f,\n                \"provider '{}' RPM limit exceeded ({}/min)\",\n                provider, requests_per_minute\n            ),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Token Bucket (file-based)\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// On-disk token bucket state for RPM limiting.\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct TokenBucket {\n    /// Current available tokens (fractional for smooth refill).\n    pub tokens: f64,\n    /// Maximum tokens (= requests_per_minute).\n    pub capacity: u32,\n    /// Last time tokens were refilled.\n    pub last_refill: DateTime<Utc>,\n}\n\nimpl TokenBucket {\n    pub(crate) fn new(capacity: u32) -> Self {\n        TokenBucket {\n            tokens: capacity as f64,\n            capacity,\n            last_refill: Utc::now(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Refill tokens based on elapsed time since last refill.\n    fn refill(&mut self) {\n        let now = Utc::now();\n        let elapsed_secs = (now - self.last_refill).num_milliseconds().max(0) as f64 / 1000.0;\n        let refill_rate = self.capacity as f64 / 60.0; // tokens per second\n        self.tokens = (self.tokens + elapsed_secs * refill_rate).min(self.capacity as f64);\n        self.last_refill = now;\n    }\n\n    /// Try to consume one token. Returns true if successful.\n    fn try_consume(&mut self) -> bool {\n        self.refill();\n        if self.tokens >= 1.0 {\n            self.tokens -= 1.0;\n            true\n        } else {\n            false\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// RateLimiter\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Enforces provider/model concurrency limits and RPM rate limiting.\npub struct RateLimiter {\n    config: LimitsConfig,\n    /// Directory for token bucket state files (`~/.needle/state/rate_limits/`).\n    state_dir: PathBuf,\n}\n\nimpl RateLimiter {\n    /// Create a rate limiter with the given config and state directory.\n    pub fn new(config: LimitsConfig, state_dir: &Path) -> Self {\n        RateLimiter {\n            config,\n            state_dir: state_dir.join(\"rate_limits\"),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check all rate limits before dispatching.\n    ///\n    /// Returns `Allowed` if dispatch can proceed, or a specific reason why not.\n    /// The caller should back off and retry if not allowed.\n    pub fn check(\n        &self,\n        provider: Option<&str>,\n        model: Option<&str>,\n        registry: &Registry,\n    ) -> Result<RateLimitDecision> {\n        // Check provider concurrency.\n        if let Some(provider_name) = provider {\n            if let Some(provider_limits) = self.config.providers.get(provider_name) {\n                if let Some(max_concurrent) = provider_limits.max_concurrent {\n                    let decision =\n                        self.check_provider_concurrency(provider_name, max_concurrent, registry)?;\n                    if !decision.is_allowed() {\n                        return Ok(decision);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check model concurrency.\n        if let Some(model_name) = model {\n            if let Some(model_limits) = self.config.models.get(model_name) {\n                if let Some(max_concurrent) = model_limits.max_concurrent {\n                    let decision =\n                        self.check_model_concurrency(model_name, max_concurrent, registry)?;\n                    if !decision.is_allowed() {\n                        return Ok(decision);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check RPM.\n        if let Some(provider_name) = provider {\n            if let Some(provider_limits) = self.config.providers.get(provider_name) {\n                if let Some(rpm) = provider_limits.requests_per_minute {\n                    let decision = self.check_rpm(provider_name, rpm)?;\n                    if !decision.is_allowed() {\n                        return Ok(decision);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(RateLimitDecision::Allowed)\n    }\n\n    /// Check provider concurrency against the worker registry.\n    fn check_provider_concurrency(\n        &self,\n        provider: &str,\n        max_concurrent: u32,\n        registry: &Registry,\n    ) -> Result<RateLimitDecision> {\n        let workers = registry.list()?;\n        let active_count = workers\n            .iter()\n            .filter(|w| w.provider.as_deref() == Some(provider))\n            .count() as u32;\n\n        if active_count >= max_concurrent {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::ProviderConcurrencyExceeded {\n                provider: provider.to_string(),\n                current: active_count,\n                limit: max_concurrent,\n            })\n        } else {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::Allowed)\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check model concurrency against the worker registry.\n    fn check_model_concurrency(\n        &self,\n        model: &str,\n        max_concurrent: u32,\n        registry: &Registry,\n    ) -> Result<RateLimitDecision> {\n        let workers = registry.list()?;\n        let active_count = workers\n            .iter()\n            .filter(|w| w.model.as_deref() == Some(model))\n            .count() as u32;\n\n        if active_count >= max_concurrent {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::ModelConcurrencyExceeded {\n                model: model.to_string(),\n                current: active_count,\n                limit: max_concurrent,\n            })\n        } else {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::Allowed)\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check RPM via a file-based token bucket.\n    fn check_rpm(&self, provider: &str, rpm: u32) -> Result<RateLimitDecision> {\n        if rpm == 0 {\n            return Ok(RateLimitDecision::Allowed);\n        }\n\n        let allowed = self.try_acquire_rpm_token(provider, rpm)?;\n        if allowed {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::Allowed)\n        } else {\n            Ok(RateLimitDecision::RpmExceeded {\n                provider: provider.to_string(),\n                requests_per_minute: rpm,\n            })\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Try to acquire an RPM token from the file-based token bucket.\n    ///\n    /// Uses flock for cross-process safety.\n    fn try_acquire_rpm_token(&self, provider: &str, rpm: u32) -> Result<bool> {\n        // Ensure the rate_limits directory exists.\n        std::fs::create_dir_all(&self.state_dir).with_context(|| {\n            format!(\n                \"failed to create rate_limits directory: {}\",\n                self.state_dir.display()\n            )\n        })?;\n\n        let bucket_path = self.state_dir.join(format!(\"{provider}.json\"));\n\n        // Open or create the bucket file.\n        let file = std::fs::OpenOptions::new()\n            .read(true)\n            .write(true)\n            .create(true)\n            .truncate(false)\n            .open(&bucket_path)\n            .with_context(|| {\n                format!(\n                    \"failed to open rate limit bucket: {}\",\n                    bucket_path.display()\n                )\n            })?;\n\n        // Exclusive lock for atomic read-modify-write.\n        FileExt::lock_exclusive(&file).with_context(|| {\n            format!(\n                \"failed to acquire lock on rate limit bucket: {}\",\n                bucket_path.display()\n            )\n        })?;\n\n        // Read current state.\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&bucket_path).unwrap_or_default();\n        let mut bucket: TokenBucket = if content.trim().is_empty() {\n            TokenBucket::new(rpm)\n        } else {\n            serde_json::from_str(&content).unwrap_or_else(|_| TokenBucket::new(rpm))\n        };\n\n        // Update capacity if config changed.\n        bucket.capacity = rpm;\n\n        // Try to consume a token.\n        let allowed = bucket.try_consume();\n\n        // Write updated state.\n        let json = serde_json::to_string_pretty(&bucket)\n            .context(\"failed to serialize token bucket state\")?;\n        std::fs::write(&bucket_path, &json).with_context(|| {\n            format!(\n                \"failed to write rate limit bucket: {}\",\n                bucket_path.display()\n            )\n        })?;\n\n        // Release lock.\n        FileExt::unlock(&file).with_context(|| {\n            format!(\n                \"failed to release lock on rate limit bucket: {}\",\n                bucket_path.display()\n            )\n        })?;\n\n        Ok(allowed)\n    }\n\n    /// Check system resource health (CPU load and memory).\n    ///\n    /// Returns warnings as log messages; does not block dispatch.\n    pub fn check_system_resources(cpu_load_warn: f64, memory_free_warn_mb: u64) {\n        // CPU load: read /proc/loadavg on Linux.\n        if let Ok(loadavg) = std::fs::read_to_string(\"/proc/loadavg\") {\n            if let Some(load_str) = loadavg.split_whitespace().next() {\n                if let Ok(load) = load_str.parse::<f64>() {\n                    // Normalize by number of CPUs.\n                    let num_cpus = std::thread::available_parallelism()\n                        .map(|n| n.get() as f64)\n                        .unwrap_or(1.0);\n                    let normalized = load / num_cpus;\n                    if normalized > cpu_load_warn {\n                        tracing::warn!(\n                            load_1min = %load_str,\n                            normalized = %format!(\"{:.2}\", normalized),\n                            threshold = %format!(\"{:.2}\", cpu_load_warn),\n                            \"CPU load exceeds warning threshold\"\n                        );\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Memory: read /proc/meminfo on Linux.\n        if let Ok(meminfo) = std::fs::read_to_string(\"/proc/meminfo\") {\n            let mut mem_available_kb: Option<u64> = None;\n            for line in meminfo.lines() {\n                if line.starts_with(\"MemAvailable:\") {\n                    if let Some(val) = line.split_whitespace().nth(1) {\n                        mem_available_kb = val.parse().ok();\n                    }\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n            if let Some(avail_kb) = mem_available_kb {\n                let avail_mb = avail_kb / 1024;\n                if avail_mb < memory_free_warn_mb {\n                    tracing::warn!(\n                        available_mb = avail_mb,\n                        threshold_mb = memory_free_warn_mb,\n                        \"available memory below warning threshold\"\n                    );\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Tests\n//    }\n    }\n\n    #[test]\n    fn no_limits_configured_allows_all() {\n        let dir = tempfile::tempdir().unwrap();\n        let registry = Registry::new(dir.path());\n        let limiter = The emitter is non-blocking: events are queued and written by a\n//! background task. A broken sink never blocks or panics the worker.\n//!\n//! ## Architecture\n//! ```text\n//! worker → emit() → mpsc::Sender → [background task] → TelemetryBus → Vec<Box<dyn Sink>>\n//! ```\n//!\n//!       }\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    bead_id = %bead.id,\n                    error = %e,\n                    \"failed to release orphaned in-progress bead\"\n                );\n                let _ = telemetry.emit(EventKind::MendBeadReleaseFailed {\n                    bead_id: bead.id.to_string(),\n                    assignee: assignee.clone(),\n                    error: e.to_string(),\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    Ok(released)\n}\n\n/// Summary of work performed during one Mend evaluation cycle.\n#[derive(Debug, Default)]\nstruct MendSummary {\n    beads_released: u32,\n    locks_removed: u32,\n    deps_cleaned: u32,\n    db_repaired: bool,\n    db_rebuilt: bool,\n    agent_logs_cleaned: u32,\n    traces_pruned: u32,\n    traces_cleaned: u32,\n    learnings_pruned: u32,\n    learnings_consolidated: u32,\n    orphaned_heartbeats_removed: u32,\n    workers_deregistered: u32,\n    idle_workers_flagged: u32,\n    rate_limits_cleaned: u32,\n    rate_limit_providers_removed: u32,\n    rate_limit_providers_reset: u32,\n}\n\nimpl MendSummary {\n    /// Whether mend performed work that changes bead store state.\n    ///\n    /// Only operations that add or release claimable beads should return true.\n    /// A strand MUST return `WorkCreated` only when it inserts a claimable bead\n    /// into the store that the waterfall will re-scan. No-op cleanup (pruning\n    /// traces, removing stale locks, repairing DB) should return `NoWork`.\n    ///\n    /// Operations that return `WorkCreated`:\n    /// - `beads_released > 0`: Orphaned beads were released back to Open status.\n    /// - `deps_cleaned > 0`: Stale dependency links were removed (beads become claimable).\n    ///\n    /// Operations that return `NoWork` (maintenance, not work creation):\n    /// - `locks_removed > 0`: Lock file cleanup (doesn't add beads to queue).\n    /// - `db_repaired`: Doctor repair fixed index corruption (doesn't add beads).\n    /// - `db_rebuilt`: Full rebuild from JSONL (doesn't add beads).\n    /// - `traces_pruned`, `agent_logs_cleaned`, `learnings_*`: File cleanup.\n    ///\n    /// A `WorkCreated` return must be paired with a telemetry event identifying\n    /// the created bead(s) so operators can see what the restart is chasing.\n    fn did_work(&self) -> bool {\n        // Bead release and dependency removal add claimable items to the queue.\n        // Lock removal, DB repair, and DB rebuild are maintenance operations\n        // that don't create new work and must not trigger a waterfall restart.\n        self.beads_released > 0 || self.deps_cleaned > 0\n    }\n}\n\n/// The Mend strand — maintenance and self-healing.\npub struct MendStrand {\n    config: MendConfig,\n    heartbeat_dir: PathBuf,\n    heartbeat_ttl: Duration,\n    lock_dir: PathBuf,\n    /// Fully-qualified worker identity ({adapter}-{worker_id}).\n    /// Used for heartbeat file lookups and registry comparisons to prevent\n    /// `trace_retention_success_days`: retention days for successful bead traces\n    /// - `workspace`: workspace root path for learning consolidation\n    /// - `max_learnings`: maximum number of learning entries before consolidation\n    /// - `state_dir`: base state directory (contains `rate_limits/` subdirectory)\n    /// - `limits_config`: provider/model limits configuration for rate limiter cleanup\n    #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]\n    pub fn new(\n        config: MendConfig,\n        heartbeat_dir: PathBuf,\n        heartbeat_ttl: Duration,\n        lock_dir: PathBuf,\n registry,\n            telemetry,\n            log_dir,\n            retention_days,\n            traces_dir,\n            trace_retention_failed_days,\n            trace_retention_success_days,\n            workspace,\n            max_learnings,\n            state_dir,\n            limits_config,\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ── Step 1: Stale claim cleanup via peer monitoring MendSummary,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        let peer_monitor = PeerMonitor::new(\n            self.heartbeat_dir.clone(),\n            self.heartbeat_ttl,\n            self.qualified_id.clone(),\n            store,\n            &self.registry,\n            self.telemetry.clone(),\n        );\n\n        let peer_result = peer_monitor.check_peers().await?;\n        summary.beads_released += peer_result.beads_released;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    // ── Step 1.5: Orphaned in-progress bead recovery ────────────────────────\n\n    /// Scan all in-progress beads and release any whose Full rebuild (rm .beads/beads.db + br sync --import + verify)\n    ///\n    /// If the full rebuild also fails, the JSONL itself may be corrupt.\n    async fn check_db_health(\n        &self,\n        store: &dyn BeadStore,\n        summary: &mut MendSummary,\n    ) -> Result<()> {\n        // Step 1: Probe with `br doctor` (no repair).\n        let check_result = store.doctor_check().await;\n\n        let needs_repair = match check_result {\n            Ok(report) => {\n                // Doctor succeeded. If there are warnings, escalate to repair.\n                !report.warnings.is_empty()\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                let msg = format!(\"{e:#}\");\n                if crate::bead_store::is_corruption_error(&msg) {\n                    tracing::warn!(error = %e, \"br doctor detected corruption\");\n                    true\n                } else {\n                    // Non-corruption error (e.g., br not found). escalating to full rebuild\"\n                    );\n                } else {\n                    // No warnings and no fixes - DB is clean, no work needed.\n                    return Ok(());\n                }\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::warn!(\n                    error = %e,\n                    \"br doctor --repair failed, attempting full rebuild\"\n                );\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Step 3: Full rebuild — rm db + br sync --import + verify.\n        match store.full_rebuild().await {\n            Ok(()) => {\n                tracing::info!(\"database fully rebuilt from JSONL\");\n\n                let _ = self.telemetry.emit(EventKind::MendDbRebuilt);\n\n                summary.db_rebuilt = true;\n                Ok(())\n            }\n            Err(e) => {\n                tracing::error!(\n                    error = %e,\n                    \"full database rebuild failed — JSONL may be corrupt\"\n
